 polonium-210 kahalaane vaale is zehar kii jaanch bharat main mumkin nahin he

 darasal ye ek radioective tatv he
 The radiation that emanates can rapidly destroy the internal organs of the human body as well as the DNA and immune system

 Polonium-210 was discovered in 1898 by the scientist Marie Curie, who gave radium to the world

 yadi ye khaane ke saath milakar insaani sharir main jaae to iskaa swaad tak pataa nahin lagaaya ja saktaa
